They fell behind by as many as 22 points in the second quarter before managing to gain some ground and closing to within 53-40 at halftime. ''I'm really proud of this group's resilience and their ability to fight and continue to play no matter what's happening in the game,'' Magic coach Jamahl Mosley said.
